<p>Initialism of its component <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beschikking.html>beschikking</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stelling.html>stelling</a></i>. Because the initialism <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more common than the full form, it can be considered to be an anacronym.

***tc.html

***td.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> td (11072)</h1><br></body> 
***te.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> (21)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>too <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating excess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">too much <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never good</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gek.html>gek</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">far out!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">modifying an infinitive verb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>Er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eten.html>eten</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> something to eat</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>located at, in, on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a></b> Amsterdam</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">in Amsterdam.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijden.html>rijden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">and so <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> ride on horseback.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in idiom; a form of the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>Te</a> drommel</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">by <a href = vnd.unilang:jove.html>Jove</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This preposition used to govern the dative case. It also fused with the dative forms of the definite article:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a></span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a></span> for feminine singular.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">at, in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">ten</span> = <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> + <span class="Latn" lang="nl">den</span> in all other <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a>.</li></ul>
<p>Combinations with the nominative form of the article, like *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> or *<i><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> have never become part of the language. The collapse of the inflection system and the related demise of the distinction between masculine and feminine gender (for most <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pushed.html>pushed</a> this preposition into partial disuse. It does however occur in a fair number of idiomatic expressions, often with fossilized case <a href = vnd.unilang:endings.html>endings</a>, e.g.:
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> elfder <a href = vnd.unilang:ure.html>ure</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the eleventh hour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigen.html>eigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bate.html>bate</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for one's own profit</span></div></dd></dl>
<p>(<i>Elfder</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ure.html>ure</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bate.html>bate</a></i> are dative forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:elfde.html>elfde</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baat.html>baat</a></i> respectively.)
</p>
<hr />

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> gebruikmaking <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>, per, <a href = vnd.unilang:middels.html>middels</a>.
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>Komt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voet.html>voet</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:paard.html>paard</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fiets.html>fiets</a>?</i> </li>

<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beveel.html>beveel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a>.</i> </li>

<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duidelijk.html>duidelijk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:vanouds.html>Vanouds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <i><a href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/datief" class="extiw" title="w:datief">datief</a></i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:techniek.html>techniek</a> (3842)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">technique</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τεχνικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tekhnikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of or pertaining to art, artistic, skilful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέχνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tékhnē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">art, handicraft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τίκτειν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tíktein</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bring forth, produce</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***teder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a> (11924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">teeder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tidar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tidaraz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">German Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fine; delicate; thin; sensitive; tender; weak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tear</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weak; not strong</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tidder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>tederder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">tederst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delicate, dainty</li>
<li>sensitive, tender, easily hurt or damaged</li>
<li>gentle, tender, with care
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tilde.html>tilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hield.html>hield</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> palm <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> hand.</i>
<dl><dd>He raised her up and <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> her <b>tenderly</b> in the palm of his hand.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">teve</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tiva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tibō-</i>.
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tife</i> and probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zibbe</i>.

***teer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a> (10479)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tar</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têer</i>, alternative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têder</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">têeder</i> (whence modern <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teder.html>teder</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tidar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tidaraz</i>; cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">teere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>tenderness</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teerder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">teerst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tender, delicate</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">first-person singular present indicative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></i></span></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">  imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>Over</a> time, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also used to refer to tuberculosis, analogously to English consumption.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the act of digesting or being consumed</li>
<li>tuberculosis</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology 5</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tree</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*trio</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*treo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trewą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree, wood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Pre-Germanic *<i>dréu̯om</i>, thematic e-grade derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dóru</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tree</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">træ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teren.html>teren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teer.html>teertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tree</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a> (48359)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">terne</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">double three</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dissimilated with the suffix <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerlingen.html>teerlingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerlinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">dice</span>, polyhedron used in games of chance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In modern language, only used as a part of fixed phrase '<b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:teerling.html>teerling</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geworpen.html>geworpen</a>'</b> (<i>the <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> cast</i>).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegel.html>tegel</a> (32985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tigele</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegel.html>tegel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tegela</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tigulǭ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tegula</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Ziegel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tile</i>.

***tegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> (132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tjegen</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> jegen</i>, the latter from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">gegin</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*gagin</i>. See also <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jegens.html>jegens</a></i>.
</p>

***tegenbericht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenbericht.html>tegenbericht</a> (98958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bericht.html>bericht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">message</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegenbericht.html>tegenbericht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegenbericht.html>tegenberichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegenbericht.html>tegenberichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>message in response, response</li>

<p>Compouund of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:offensief.html>offensief</a></i>. The entered common usage during the First World War.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenpartij.html>tegenpartij</a> (17954)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">against, counter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partij</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">party, group</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***tegenvaller.html

<p>root of <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenvallen.html>tegenvallen</a> 'to go adversely' (from tegen- 'against' + <a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a> 'to fall') + <a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>A disappointing result, adversity, bummer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegenwerping.html>tegenwerping</a> (98947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***tehuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a> (7458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> huus</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuizen.html>tehuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>home, asylum</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Whereas <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:thuis.html>thuis</a></i> refers to one's home as a place of residence, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:tehuis.html>tehuis</a></i> refers to an asylum or refuge where one may or may not feel at home.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bejaardentehuis.html>bejaardentehuis</a></span></li></ul>

</p>
